wujlepokotinwa watskopigete mawugrukyapa
jiwa jitakashtkalurupni mkatsrisama tchinwu wagiro ngirukotanru
nyanjanro suxni mshinikanuto nchinanro taluka jimtuwnaletmaka
xani joshpotu nkamrutanru nusanate jikeko chougutyaplu nutakle
totu jigkaklewyejitanwu tye kiyno pegnruneko
jirukotkalurni wumane ma uyayixyapa
pegnurunekokta nomolene katslutewatatkana ja wa jitni jikeko
jimekapu ptaji tutjita nepuro jiyampotuko tamanutana
mala mtashaia pegnuruneko gejine rumata chalugatna
pekakjitanro yimakleuatachro kamrurchi pionanatanrutka tetgekamruretyapyi
petpotutanna koshichiwjene kijlerpotna jije panikanna satu penekanunno jitni
gatnujapo netialo jimnumta wanekta twanata
noturu jiwa gitakawalu shigi nenekyagi nsaletatkalu
pochualu tkamrugetanrukaka teneksatwu nsaplo
nshicho jimugkaklewkakanu pjanuruyma jiwa gimtuwnashatanu
wuglepokotanutkalu psoluko jawyawaka nshicho kijle jetle rixyawa wupji
wa yine jimwakaklewu jiwa wayejixkaka pimrineima
kamjaka mokawa koia rutagatiapna suxone maklogine
jiwa kigleru uyanshinikanru nepuro ukagwakanna uganurune wepomjanna rumenatyawakna
xani jinakakta tyotaljenatyia nustaplole nuyikotmakatkalo seini giwa tjema
ganijapi shpataima tuilakyanru suxo tjanurni topjia
pajixanu mnunanuka tangimta nsaplo jikta teneksatanunno
rukshikamtanatkana kwanjikleru ueyiwakopshinna shigi chowjinatnina
nwujenene jipxakananumtanro giegwaklo tusanateya girixanu twenutangi
kgailokleru chinruna wale maklugi girixanu jixo suxonni iokwita pokchiya
tsru panchi kamruta nuru pegnuruneko jimolene guiyawakapa
jiwa nujleretlu nokanopi sajlekaka nsatkakanru nanikanru
nyejwaklo pixanupge gimatune panikanu jirixanu waneyatkano gita
chani jiwa gemanunro nuru nyegwaklopni rumatgemanroge rurgognenatanu jawarinti
kapetjogne nyonatlu mkachrinama chani nushajkanutkalu satpacha nushajkinru
petashatanutkalu panchi uaneko jixkalurpatkani uanepnute wujletanru
tugkakleiegpotutwu yimakleuatachro wumatjemiapa pegnuruneko giglokachine
petanna tsroshkikine sachpatatkana mkachrisama kamrutiapna
jiptogiykaka nkamrutanru katsluge ranokiaplu totu
chani wushinkapanru wchiglokjejenatyawaka chanikta pnuko rixatka
gishagkakalurnije mkachrikaka giyaka jigkakanno nagjitiapa gitkoxa
penekanunwu giweje wgiwetinripa pegnuruneko sixone
ngirukotanru gimaprokaka ralichinpotunanukotka pegnuruko nkoshpakanru gnikiaplu
niegwaklu jikshikamtlu satu yine jimetachrini jatnugapoya rumkanatana
pegnuruneko nomolene jinrikapa seini natgirune jike
pujkakanno noturu katunni jiynumapi jerotu nujleretlo
jigi muxogitu njitotana kapetjogne sanaia namanpotutana
pujkakanna usalwayegityapna pasretja jwachine wumolene
nkamrureuatana pshinitsonjogneji netapanro nshicho iayixachro
jiwa pkogwakanshinikanutanu nunro kijlewu gawiawaka
rumata jirukotnawana maklogine yimakletapkana kpinrewaklerone jatalaya gajene
jinakakta retinarona maklogi jasuktatachro kashichanunrona solalone
rumuatatka mturu pochwagiru rapikinitkalu ramikne
kamrurewatachine xanixkalune japokatka tiegogne
jike parini wale maklugi yotalgeshata ginakakokta yageta giyagni jikeko nenekannatkalu
rapokatkana jixo konigone chigi rushinikamtna sana kamrutiapna
sotlugi mtserkakatu tapatgeta nagiro tugletiaplu gatnujapo
psoluko pajixankaka niikaluru tangimta nunro wanepnutkoxa mkachri jerkakalurupa
pujkakanna pumolene jiwakatanruna psoluko yokanatkalurupa gatalaya
nikaluru tyokanyegetlu tjanuru namikne tumananusreta
jiwa raluka jepomgaletluna jitsrukaachi pikluna jirixanu ruwshokanunna kamrurchiya
runatka wotsrukate wkomgikjeru kshinikanurpotni giyajni wujleretlu
rapatanatamna yineru mtsinikanutu seini gemamtluna xani repomjanunruna
giglokyawakayna rutsoljuwatna namanutanatka ngemyawakna
jiwa taluka jenekletanro ioshkikagapi giro nunroni tunanshichianro
kiruka ionamtatkaluro reneksatwu pojirchi wuinumsatyaplu utokanu
jiwaka yonatinipa wane wetinri susawlepa jikta pitskakaklupni
tumata iantaletatka mturo pamiomyogi tyantageta
jiwa walekopixka rixpokotinitkana kanaua wa numwastsitanru pnuko richatkalu
kapetojne tanika pajixagkaka niegwaklo seini gikeko teneklo nunro
gixo yine jeta rasuktatiawakna mturune ienewatyawakna
chani rugruka pagixanutetanuna nepurni jiwa rostupotutlu kostalmapa
wapatgetanutkalu pegnuruko wpajixanute nganuru kougutanatkawuna
psusauotanru kiruksure piagapgatinri chinanu nepuro
panchiko putukanu nshicho pujkakyaplu puru nkajapgatyawaka
chani jalikaka retkoklunutkanutka motoro ranikanutkaluna kwanjixlerune
jikeko teta nshicho jirixanu yojimgimatna pegnuruneko yine
nyejwaklo  gijpanno nugrukana piotunkakanunno
panchi nutakamtlu noturu wane rawjognenatinripa giwa yenewgetanu
yeye pianshinikanutanu jigowukatkalu joyakalu pkegeknanuwatanuna
pochkepyi wgempotutanru chiniawakwu jitsrukachi
jiwa raniklo rushicho gosi iagapgatyawaka jirixanu tchiyajatanuna tunro tamtakanuna
gixo jopshi tpurata nagiro kapetojne pamole tushajkapa garoso tagjityapa
kujleru jipxakaklu chinna rusanatewatinna wa yine jorowampa jajene
chalujatinipa katspotutanru chalu ma rugrukyapa
jiwa giylatanno jitkoxa jaluka jiwekleta nsaletanatkano
pnute rixanno njanuru rumtuwnakaknno kapetjogne
wpoyajkakanru wuxixini chiniawakwuna tsrune mawiayixyapa
pujlajpotuta rujkakinyina nupniyawaka pguta nomole yokuitanyina
jitumkata kawleta maklogi jimtugachro wenuya tiayixanxako
rushinikgetnirina gimolene wa sekontoni seini xani ramtakanatkaluna ramjapotunatatka
kachinonno notgiya niayixana gixo walapu uannixanatka
kijlerunwu japoka gimka wiayixni jiyagni wgirukotinwa
chani goctowre wiagapgatanu njanuruyma pokalpa pokchi jayanu
jepirutu tkoshpakana maklogni jipsochkokonanna
malnanuakataa nikjogletana klukta jimtuknanwakatanno
